RACE OVERVIEW
=============
The 2024 Formula 1 Singapore Grand Prix was held on September 22, 2024, at the Marina Bay Street Circuit. Lando Norris of McLaren secured pole position and went on to win the race, leading every lap. Max Verstappen of Red Bull Racing finished second, and Oscar Piastri, also of McLaren, completed the podium in third. The race was notable as the fastest Singapore Grand Prix and the first to not feature a safety car or yellow flag period. Only two retirements occurred during the race with Alexander Albon and Kevin Magnussen retiring in the pits. Daniel Ricciardo set the fastest lap, although he did not receive the bonus point as he finished outside the top ten.
